//<![CDATA[

var browserHeight = function() {
    var myHeight = 0;
    if( typeof( window.innerHeight ) == 'number' ) {
        myHeight = window.innerHeight;
    } else if( document.documentElement && document.documentElement.clientHeight ) {
        myHeight = document.documentElement.clientHeight;
    } else if( document.body && document.body.clientHeight ) {
        myHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
    }
    return myHeight;
};

function focusCommentBox() {
        var cmtObject = document.getElementById('write_commet_box');
        if(cmtObject === null || cmtObject === undefined ) {
            var resultDiv = document.getElementById('cmt_info');
            var message = resultDiv.getAttribute("data-message");
            if(message !== null || message !== '') {
                alert(message);
            }
        } else {
            var size = cmtObject.getHeight() + cmtObject.offsetTop + 20;
            var height = browserHeight();
            var result = size - height;
            result = (result > 0 ) ? result: 0;

            window.scrollTo(0, result);
        }

}
